FNV GRAPHICS EFFECT PHASE CONTRACT AUDIT

Questions:
1. Is there a stable non-invasive boundary after first-person rendering and before vanilla image-space?
2. Does the current post-world/pre-image-space milestone avoid known graphics-mod collision sites?
3. Which vanilla calls overwrite or consume render targets after each candidate scene phase?
4. Which DepthResolve, Shader Loader, and TESReloaded-style sites should stay opt-in or off-limits?

Static limitation:
This script cannot see runtime detours from loaded DLLs. It proves vanilla code shape and known static collision areas only.

======================================================================
PHASE CONTRACT NOTES
======================================================================
Current conservative milestone:
  scene_pre_image_space runs after Main::RenderWorldSceneGraph returns, only on is_first_person == 0.
  This avoids DepthResolve-owned sites and first-person depth-clear patches, but it is before weapon rendering.
  It is expected to fix AO over far fog for world geometry, not to solve every first-person composition issue.

Boundary to prove before moving deeper:
  The ideal non-invasive scene boundary is after first-person geometry and before ProcessImageSpaceShaders.
  If that boundary is only available as a narrow callsite, prefer a targeted callsite hook over broad native replacement.

Off-limits by default:
  DepthResolve-owned GetDepthTexture and replacement callsites.
  TESReloaded-style first-person depth-clear patch.
  Native shader creation hooks unless an opt-in compatibility mode is selected.
